Spotify's censorship in response to social trends is also troublesome since social trends constantly shift and, especially recently, become more authoritarian. If the message is truly egregious, demonetizing music is an option. Demonetization is only hostile to the artist, whereas outright censorship is hostile to artist and customer. We should be free to choose how we use the service and to be secured when Spotify's security is eventually compromised.
